<h1 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center mainh1 has-large-font-size"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Jenny_Mod"></span><strong>Jenny Mod</strong><span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h1>



<p class="has-text-align-center">JennyMod.co is the official website of Jenny Mod. Get your virtual girlfriend in the Minecraft universe with us. Download Jenny Mod Java &amp; Bedrock MCPE Editions.</p>



<p class="has-text-align-center vv has-medium-font-size">v<strong>1.12.2</strong></p>



<p class="has-text-align-center btnn"><a href="#dl">DOWNLOAD NOW</a></p>
</div></div>



<div style="height:19px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div>



<p>Are you looking for a virtual girlfriend in the Minecraft universe? Look no further than the Jenny Mod.</p>



<p><a href="https://jennymod.co/">Jenny Mod</a> is an addon that adds a virtual girlfriend to your Minecraft world. With this mod, you can customise the look of your virtual girlfriend, communicate, and do whatever you want with her in-game as you do in real life.</p>



<p>But if you have no idea how to download, install, use, or what features Jenny Mod has, then you’re in the right place.</p>



<p>In this article, we will provide a <strong>Jenny Mod download</strong> guide along with all the necessary information you need to know about Jenny Mod. So let&#8217;s get started.</p>

<p>Jenny Mod is a <a href="https://www.minecraft.net/" rel="nofollow noopener">Minecraft</a> addon mod created by SlipperyTum in 2018. It is a custom add-on that lets players have a virtual girlfriend in their Minecraft world.</p>



<p>Also, note that Jenny is just the addon name, but you can name anything to your virtual girlfriends, like Jenny, Slime Girl, Bee, Ellie, Luna, Kobolds, Allie, and Goblins.</p>



<p>Minecraft is a virtual world, and Jenny Mod will help you build your own virtual world with your girlfriend. That&#8217;s why people are so interested in this mod.</p>



<p>For Minecraft, you can get several modded apps and add-ons to customise the look of your virtual environment. But Jenny Mod is one of the best mod add-ons if you are looking for a virtual girlfriend.</p>



<p>She can do whatever you want her to and look however you want her to. You can customise your virtual girlfriend&#8217;s size, shape, colour, skin tone, and more to make her look the way you want.</p>



<p>You can also take her to dinner, a party, a dance, or even on a date. You can also have her do any other activities a real girlfriend would do.</p>

<figure class="aligncenter size-full is-resized"><img decoding="async" width="512" height="512" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20512%20512'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="no-ads" class="wp-image-88" style="object-fit:contain;width:90px;height:90px" data-lazy-srcset="https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/no-ads.webp 512w, https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/no-ads-300x300.webp 300w, https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/no-ads-150x150.webp 150w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 512px) 100vw, 512px" data-lazy-src="https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/no-ads.webp" /><noscript><img decoding="async" width="512" height="512" src="https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/no-ads.webp" alt="no-ads" class="wp-image-88" style="object-fit:contain;width:90px;height:90px" srcset="https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/no-ads.webp 512w, https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/no-ads-300x300.webp 300w, https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/no-ads-150x150.webp 150w" sizes="(max-width: 512px) 100vw, 512px" /></noscript></figure>
</div>


<h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="No_Ads"></span><strong>No Ads</strong><span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3>



<p>You don&#8217;t have to worry about annoying ads as the Jenny Mod is totally ad-free.</p>
</div>
</div>



<p>These are some of the features you can access with Jenny Mod addons, even in the official version. If you use the Minecraft modded version like Bedrock, you can get much more from these mod add-ons.</p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="All_Characters"></span>All Characters<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h2>



<p>As someone who&#8217;s spent <em>way too much time</em> exploring every corner of the Jenny Mod world (and loving every second of it), I’ve compiled this complete list of all the amazing characters you’ll meet in the mod. Each one brings something unique, from combat help to magical mischief, and yep… some pretty fun adult interactions too.</p>



<div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-9d6595d7 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-column characters-section is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
<div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-9d6595d7 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-column character is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Jenny"></span>Jenny<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large is-resized"><img decoding="async" width="683" height="1024" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20683%201024'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Jenny-Character-Image" class="wp-image-359" style="width:200px" data-lazy-srcset="https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Image-683x1024.webp 683w, https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Image-200x300.webp 200w, https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Image-768x1152.webp 768w, https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Image.webp 1024w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 683px) 100vw, 683px" data-lazy-src="https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Image-683x1024.webp" /><noscript><img decoding="async" width="683" height="1024" src="https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Image-683x1024.webp" alt="Jenny-Character-Image" class="wp-image-359" style="width:200px" srcset="https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Image-683x1024.webp 683w, https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Image-200x300.webp 200w, https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Image-768x1152.webp 768w, https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Image.webp 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 683px) 100vw, 683px" /></noscript></figure>
</div>


<p>The original girl and the mod&#8217;s face. Jenny isn’t just cute, she’s smart, teleporting like an Enderman, healing herself, and even helping you out in battles. She’s fully interactive, which is why this mod went viral.</p>
</div>



<div class="wp-block-column character is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Ellie"></span>Ellie<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large is-resized"><img decoding="async" width="683" height="1024" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20683%201024'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Jenny-Character-Ellie-Image" class="wp-image-358" style="width:200px" data-lazy-srcset="https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Ellie-Image-683x1024.webp 683w, https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Ellie-Image-200x300.webp 200w, https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Ellie-Image-768x1152.webp 768w, https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Ellie-Image.webp 1024w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 683px) 100vw, 683px" data-lazy-src="https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Ellie-Image-683x1024.webp" /><noscript><img decoding="async" width="683" height="1024" src="https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Ellie-Image-683x1024.webp" alt="Jenny-Character-Ellie-Image" class="wp-image-358" style="width:200px" srcset="https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Ellie-Image-683x1024.webp 683w, https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Ellie-Image-200x300.webp 200w, https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Ellie-Image-768x1152.webp 768w, https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Ellie-Image.webp 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 683px) 100vw, 683px" /></noscript></figure>
</div>


<p>A forest-loving companion you’ll often find in darker wooded biomes. Ellie helps you gather resources, heals you when you’re hurt, and she’s surprisingly tough in a fight.</p>
</div>
</div>



<div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-9d6595d7 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-column character is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Bee_Girl"></span>Bee Girl<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large is-resized"><img decoding="async" width="683" height="1024" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20683%201024'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Jenny-Character-Bee-Girl-Image" class="wp-image-357" style="width:200px" data-lazy-srcset="https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Bee-Girl-Image-683x1024.webp 683w, https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Bee-Girl-Image-200x300.webp 200w, https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Bee-Girl-Image-768x1152.webp 768w, https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Bee-Girl-Image.webp 1024w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 683px) 100vw, 683px" data-lazy-src="https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Bee-Girl-Image-683x1024.webp" /><noscript><img decoding="async" width="683" height="1024" src="https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Bee-Girl-Image-683x1024.webp" alt="Jenny-Character-Bee-Girl-Image" class="wp-image-357" style="width:200px" srcset="https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Bee-Girl-Image-683x1024.webp 683w, https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Bee-Girl-Image-200x300.webp 200w, https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Bee-Girl-Image-768x1152.webp 768w, https://jennymod.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/Jenny-Character-Bee-Girl-Image.webp 1024w" sizes="(max-width: 683px) 100vw, 683px" /></noscript></figure>
</div>


<p>Sweet but deadly. Bee Girl helps with farming by pollinating crops and can summon a swarm of bees to attack your enemies. She’s perfect for nature builds and village life.</p>
</div>



<div class="wp-block-column character is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Slime_Girl"></span>Slime Girl<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3>


<div class="wp-block-image">

</div>


<p>She’s squishy, she’s bubbly, and she can split into mini-slimes during combat. Slime Girl is your go-to sidekick when you want a fun and gooey companion to fight mobs with.</p>
</div>
</div>



<div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-9d6595d7 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-column character is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Allie_The_Genie_Girl"></span>Allie (The Genie Girl)<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3>


<div class="wp-block-image">

</div>


<p>Rub the lamp and poof &#8211; Allie appears! This genie girl grants three random wishes, usually in the form of rare loot or boosts. She&#8217;s rare, but totally worth finding in desert temples or strongholds.</p>
</div>



<div class="wp-block-column character is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Goblin_Girl"></span>Goblin Girl<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3>


<div class="wp-block-image">

</div>


<p>This green little troublemaker loves shiny things, especially gold. You’ll usually find her sneaking around caves and mines. Watch your loot, or she’ll snatch it and vanish!</p>
</div>
</div>



<div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-9d6595d7 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">

<div class="wp-block-image">

</div>


<p>Bia is like a magical healer. She’s calm, gentle, and protects you with health boosts and potion effects. A great companion for long exploration trips.</p>
</div>



<div class="wp-block-column character is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Luna"></span>Luna<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3>


<div class="wp-block-image">

</div>


<p>Luna is the ocean girl of the squad. She adores fish and will trade you cool items if you bring her some. If you hang out near rivers or beaches, you might be lucky enough to spot her.</p>
</div>
</div>



<div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-9d6595d7 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-column character is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Kobold_Girl"></span>Kobold Girl<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3>


<div class="wp-block-image">

</div>


<p>Half dragon, half chaos! Kobold Girl is a rare protector usually spotted near dragon dens or the End. She&#8217;s small, fierce, and loves shiny armour and you.</p>
</div>



<div class="wp-block-column character is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">

<p>Galath is a powerful Nether warrior, and sometimes you’ll even meet her fierce daughter, Manglelie. These two are boss-tier characters who can turn the tide in dangerous areas.</p>
</div>

<p>These are the 14 characters of Jenny. Every character in the Jenny Mod world has their own personality, powers, and surprises. Whether you’re building a fantasy town, going on a wild adventure, or just vibing with Jenny and her friends, this crew will keep things interesting.</p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="How_To_Download_Jenny_Mod"></span>How To Download Jenny Mod?<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h2>



<p>Downloading and installing the Jenny mod is not as easy as it seems. You need to be careful and follow each step accordingly to install the mod successfully.</p>



<p>In modded apps, you only have to enable unknown sources and download the modded version of the game.</p>



<p>For Jenny Mod, you need to download the file from an external website, then add it to Minecraft using additional tools like Forge.</p>



<p>Also, note that the Jenny Mod Java Edition is not compatible with the Bedrock version of Minecraft. It works only with the Java edition, which is available only through official Minecraft.</p>



<p>But no worries, even if you&#8217;re using the modded version of the game Bedrock, you can still install Jenny Mod with ease.</p>



<p>Below are two download links that you can use to get started:</p>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>Jenny Mod Java Edition &#8211; <strong><a href="https://jennymod.co/download/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener nofollow">Download</a></strong></li>



<li>Jenny Mod Bedrock Edition (MCPE) &#8211; <strong><a href="https://jennymod.co/jenny-mod-mcpe/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener nofollow">Download</a></strong></li>
</ul>



<p>Make sure to download the version for your Minecraft edition.</p>



<p><strong>Note</strong>: Both of these add-ons are suitable only for PC &amp; Mac.</p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="How_to_Install_Jenny_Mod_on_Minecraft_%E2%80%93_PC_Java_Edition_Mobile_MCPE"></span>How to Install Jenny Mod on Minecraft &#8211; PC (Java Edition) &amp; Mobile (MCPE)<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h2>



<p>As someone who’s been using Jenny Mod regularly, I’ve created this complete step-by-step <strong>installation guide</strong> for both <strong>PC (Java Edition)</strong> and <strong>Mobile (MCPE/Bedrock)</strong> players. Whether you&#8217;re playing on a computer or your phone, this will get you started in no time. Well, you can check out my detailed <a href="https://jennymod.co/how-to-install/">guide to install Jenny mod</a> or follow the steps given below.</p>



<div class="wp-block-columns install-section is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-9d6595d7 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-column install-section is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
<div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-9d6595d7 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-column install-pc is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading install-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="PC_Installation_Guide_Minecraft_Java_Edition"></span><strong>PC Installation Guide (Minecraft Java Edition)</strong><span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3>



<p>Jenny Mod works best on Minecraft <strong>Java Edition</strong>, especially version <strong>1.12.2</strong>. Let’s get started!</p>



<h4 class="wp-block-heading install-subhead"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Requirements"></span><strong>Requirements:</strong><span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h4>



<ul class="wp-block-list install-list">
<li>Jenny Mod <code>.jar</code> file (download it from <a href="https://jennymod.co/download/">here</a>)</li>



<li>Minecraft Java Edition is installed</li>



<li>Java is installed on your PC (version 8 or above)</li>



<li>Minecraft Forge 1.12.2 (Jenny Mod Was Developed for 1.12.2) &#8211; <a href="https://files.minecraftforge.net/net/minecraftforge/forge/index_1.12.2.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Download</a></li>
</ul>



<h4 class="wp-block-heading install-subhead"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Step-by-Step_Installation"></span><strong>Step-by-Step Installation:</strong><span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h4>



<div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-9d6595d7 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-column install-step is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
<p class="has-medium-font-size">Step 1: Install Minecraft Forge</p>



<ol class="wp-block-list">
<li>Go to Forge 1.12.2 and download the <strong>recommended installer</strong>.</li>



<li>Run the installer and select <strong>“Install Client.”</strong></li>



<li>Once installed, open the Minecraft Launcher and select the new <strong>Forge 1.12.2</strong> profile.</li>
</ol>
</div>
</div>



<div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-9d6595d7 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-column install-step is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
<p class="has-medium-font-size">Step 2: Locate Your Mods Folder</p>



<ol class="wp-block-list">
<li>Press <code>Win + R</code>, type <code>%appdata%</code> and hit Enter.</li>



<li>Navigate to: <code>\.minecraft\mods\</code></li>



<li>If you don’t see a <code>mods</code> folder, just create one manually.</li>
</ol>
</div>
</div>



<div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-9d6595d7 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-column install-step is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
<p class="has-medium-font-size">Step 3: Add Jenny Mod</p>



<ol class="wp-block-list">
<li>Download the Jenny Mod <code>.jar</code> file from <a href="https://jennymod.co/download/">jennymod.app</a>.</li>



<li>Copy and paste the file into the <code>mods</code> folder.</li>
</ol>
</div>
</div>



<div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-9d6595d7 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-column install-step is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
<p class="has-medium-font-size">Step 4: Launch the Game</p>



<ol class="wp-block-list">
<li>Open Minecraft Launcher.</li>



<li>Select the <strong>Forge 1.12.2</strong> profile and hit <strong>Play</strong>.</li>



<li>Once the game loads, you’ll find Jenny in your world! Use creative mode to spawn her via the <strong>“Jenny” egg</strong>.</li>
</ol>
</div>
</div>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading install-tip"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Tips"></span>Tips:<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>If you experience a crash, make sure <strong>you’re on version 1.12.2</strong> and no other conflicting mods are installed.</li>



<li>Always <strong>back up your worlds</strong> before installing any mod.</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>



<div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-9d6595d7 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-column install-mobile is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
<h3 class="wp-block-heading install-heading"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Mobile_Installation_Guide_Minecraft_PE_Bedrock_Edition"></span><strong>Mobile Installation Guide (Minecraft PE / Bedrock Edition)</strong><span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3>



<p>Yes! Jenny Mod can also be installed on <strong>Minecraft</strong><span style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><strong>: Pocket Edition (MCPE)</strong>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<strong>Bedrock Edition,</strong></span> especially on <strong>Android</strong>.</p>



<p>⚠️ <em>iOS support is limited and may require 3rd-party tools or jailbreaking.</em></p>



<h4 class="wp-block-heading install-subhead"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Requirements-2"></span><strong>Requirements:</strong><span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h4>



<ul class="wp-block-list install-list">
<li>Minecraft PE (Bedrock Edition 1.17+)</li>



<li>File manager app (e.g. <a href="https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=ru.zdevs.zarchiver" rel="nofollow noopener">ZArchiver</a> or <a href="https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.cxinventor.file.explorer" rel="nofollow noopener">CX File Explorer</a>)</li>



<li>Jenny Mod <code>.mcaddon</code> or <code>.mcpack</code> file (<a href="https://jennymod.co/jenny-mod-mcpe/">Download from here</a>)</li>
</ul>



<h4 class="wp-block-heading install-subhead"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Step-by-Step_Installation_Android"></span><strong>Step-by-Step Installation (Android):</strong><span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h4>



<div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-9d6595d7 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-column install-step is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
<p class="has-medium-font-size">Step 1: Download the Mod</p>



<ol class="wp-block-list">
<li>Download the <code>.mcaddon</code> file on your phone.</li>



<li>Use your file manager to locate the downloaded file.</li>
</ol>
</div>
</div>



<div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-9d6595d7 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-column install-step is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
<p class="has-medium-font-size">Step 2: Import to Minecraft</p>



<ol class="wp-block-list">
<li>Tap the <code>.mcaddon</code> file – it should open automatically in Minecraft.</li>



<li>Minecraft will launch and import the Jenny Mod pack.</li>
</ol>
</div>
</div>



<div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-9d6595d7 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-column install-step is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
<p class="has-medium-font-size">Step 3: Activate the Mod</p>



<ol class="wp-block-list">
<li>Create a new world or edit an existing one.</li>



<li>Go to:
<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li><strong>Behaviour Packs</strong> → activate <strong>Jenny Mod</strong></li>



<li><strong>Resource Packs</strong> → activate <strong>Jenny Textures</strong></li>
</ul>
</li>



<li>Scroll down and enable <strong>“Experimental Gameplay”</strong>.</li>
</ol>
</div>
</div>



<div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-9d6595d7 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-column install-step is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
<p class="has-medium-font-size">Step 4: Play the Game!</p>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>Spawn Jenny using an <strong>egg</strong> from Creative inventory.</li>



<li>Enjoy the interactions!</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>



<h4 class="wp-block-heading install-subhead"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Alternative_Method_Manual_Install"></span><strong>Alternative Method (Manual Install):</strong><span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h4>



<ol class="wp-block-list">
<li>Unzip the <code>.mcaddon</code> file.</li>



<li>Place the resource folder in:<br><code>games/com.mojang/resource_packs</code></li>



<li>Place the behaviour folder in:<br><code>games/com.mojang/behavior_packs</code></li>



<li>Follow the same world setup steps above.</li>
</ol>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading install-subhead"><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Important_Notes"></span>Important Notes:<span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h3>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>On some devices, you may need to <strong>restart Minecraft</strong> after importing.</li>



<li>The Bedrock version has <span style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><strong>fewer features</strong>&nbsp;than</span> Java.</li>



<li>For the best experience, I recommend the PC version.</li>
</ul>
</div>
